        <h2>Storyline</h2>
        
        <div class="inline canwrap">
            <p>
                <span>    Armed with the astonishing ability to shrink in scale but increase in strength, con-man Scott Lang must embrace his inner-hero and help his mentor, Dr. Hank Pym, protect the secret behind his spectacular Ant-Man suit from a new generation of towering threats. Against seemingly insurmountable obstacles, Pym and Lang must plan and pull off a heist that will save the world.</span>
                <em class="nobr">Written by
<a href="/search/title?plot_author=%40PtotheSmizzo&view=simple&sort=alpha&ref_=tt_stry_pl"
>@PtotheSmizzo</a></em>            </p>

        <h2>Did You Know?</h2>
    <div id="trivia" class="txt-block">
        <h4>Trivia</h4>
    <a href="/name/nm0339460?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Judy Greer</a> plays Maggie Lang. She also plays Karen, mother to the two boys that go to <a href="/title/tt0369610?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Jurassic World</a> (2015) on vacation where they meet Owen Grady, played by <a href="/name/nm0695435?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Chris Pratt</a> who plays Starlord/Peter Quill in <a href="/title/tt2015381?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Guardians of the Galaxy</a> (2014).        <a href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />
     <div id="goofs"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Goofs</h4>
(at around 51 mins) The crazy ants are said to be longhorn crazy ants (paratrechina longicornis) but they are actually tawny crazy ants (nylanderia fulva). Longhorn crazy ants are black in color while tawny crazy ants are red. On top of that, longhorn crazy ants aren&#39;t even attracted to electricity.        <a href="trivia?tab=gf&ref_=tt_trv_gf"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>

    <div class="article" id="titleUserReviewsTeaser">
        <h2>User Reviews</h2>
        <div class="user-comments">
                    <div class="tinystarbar" title="9/10">
                        <div style="width: 90px;">&nbsp;</div>
                    </div>
                <span>
                    <strong>I was not expecting this... Brilliant addition to the MCU.</strong>
                    <div class="comment-meta">
                        19 July 2015 | by <a href="/user/ur58672420/?ref_=tt_urv"
><span>lukehiggs</span></a>
                        &ndash; <a href="/user/ur58672420/comments?ref_=tt_urv"
>See all my reviews</a>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <p>AntMan is a lesser know character of marvels but by no means does that effect the quality of this movie. First off I thought that the casting of this film wasn&#39;t going to work, that been Paul Rudd mainly, just because I have read a few of the AntMan comics and didn&#39;t think it was going to work, I was wrong he is brilliant, hilarious and believable, all of the jokes he made actually made laugh out load which doesn&#39;t happen much. Michael Pena was great in this film, he plays the same kind of character he always seems too, but it really works, especially the story telling scenes were hilarious. This was a all round well cast film.<br/><br/>The action and CGI Was great, on first thoughts I thought when AntMan shrinks down that the CGI would take you out of the movie but let me tell you it doesn&#39;t, it&#39;s awesome! Especially seeing the world from that size and scenes where AntMan is shrinking and enlarging when fighting i thought would get a little too much but the honestly don&#39;t.<br/><br/>All around I AntMan felt different to all the other MCU movies that have come out, but a good different.    A well cast,directed and acted film that will be a welcome addition to my marvel collection.</p>
                    </div>
                </span>
                <hr />
